name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr

posted:Posted February 22, 2024
msg:This stay at the Nan'an Hilton was a very pleasant experience. When checking in, Xiao Zhang at the front desk was very attentive and asked us about our room needs. He learned that I really wanted a beautiful view, and he thoughtfully upgraded our room to a larger one with bigger windows.
Secondly, the water in the bathroom is large and the temperature is stable. When using the fixed shower head above the head, it is no exaggeration to say that I must describe it as a "waterfall". The water volume is huge, which is great.
Third, the breakfast restaurant is spacious, bright, comfortable and clean. The hotel breakfast restaurant in Putian the night before had no windows. Eating in a closed space will affect your appetite. By the way, the Hilton breakfast has a rich variety and tastes quite good, especially the fruits, which taste great.
Fourth, the entire hotel also enthusiastically promotes local culture. When you enter the room, the entire wall beside the bed is a photo of Anping Bridge. When we came to Nan'an this time, Anping Bridge was a place that I had been thinking about for four years. There is a screen on the electronic lock of every room in the hotel, which displays various famous attractions in Quanzhou. This makes me, a Quanzhou native living in Shanghai, feel warm and proud.
If there is any shortcoming, it is that there is a KTV on the lower floor of the hotel. When we went back to the room around 9pm, the vibration of the subwoofer made our heart feel very uncomfortable. We asked the hotel and they immediately moved us to the other end away from the KTV. one end. What's interesting is that before changing rooms, the subwoofer suddenly stopped, so I'm not sure whether it was the KTV that stopped the music or that I couldn't hear anything in the rooms that were changed later. However, in order to ensure quietness, it is recommended to stay in the high-rise room with the smaller room number.
